Source Code

These source-code files are part of a reconstructed copy of Artemis 071, the first release of the Apollo 15 through 17 Command Module (CM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) software.

The reconstruction began with source code of Artemis 072 previously transcribed from a digitized copy of that program. The code was then updated by undoing changes between the two versions. The reconstruction was verified by matching memory-bank checksums to those listed in drawing 2021154-. Note that page numbers in the reconstructed code match those on the Artemis 072 printout, although the changed code would likely have changed page numbers for a real Artemis 071 listing.

Comments from the original source code are prefixed with a single '#' symbol, whereas comments added later are prefixed by "##" or "###". Report any errors noted by creating an issue report at the Virtual AGC project's GitHub repository. 

001527,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
001528,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    ERASABLE_ASSIGNMENTS.agc
001529,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Artemis revision 071.
001530,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the reconstructed source code for the first
001531,000006:                                                                                                  ##              release of the flight software for the Command Module's
001532,000007:                                                                                                  ##              (CM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 15 through
001533,000008:                                                                                                  ##              17. The code has been recreated from a copy of Artemis 072.
001534,000009:                                                                                                  ##              It has been adapted such that the resulting bugger words
001535,000010:                                                                                                  ##              exactly match those specified for Artemis 071 in NASA
001536,000011:                                                                                                  ##              drawing 2021154-, which gives relatively high confidence
001537,000012:                                                                                                  ##              that the reconstruction is correct.
001538,000013:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   38
001539,000014:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
001540,000015:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
001541,000016:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
001542,000017:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2019-08-14 MAS  Created from Artemis 072.

001545,000020:                                                                                                  #  CONVENTIONS AND NOTATIONS UTILIZED FOR ERASABLE ASSIGNMENTS.
001546,000021: 
001547,000022:                                                                                                  #        EQUALS  IS USED IN TWO WAYS.  IT IS OFTEN USED TO CHAIN A GROUP
001548,000023:                                                                                                  #                OF ASSIGNMENTS SO THAT THE GROUP MAY BE MOVED WITH THE
001549,000024:                                                                                                  #                CHANGING OF ONLY ONE CARD.  EXAMPLE.
001550,000025: 
001551,000026:                                                                                                  #                                        X       EQUALS  START
001552,000027:                                                                                                  #                                        Y       EQUALS  X       +SIZE.X
001553,000028:                                                                                                  #                                        Z       EQUALS  Y       +SIZE.Y
001554,000029: 
001555,000030:                                                                                                  #                (X, Y, AND Z ARE CONSECUTIVE AND BEGIN AT START.       )
001556,000031:                                                                                                  #                (SIZE.X AND SIZE.Y ARE THE RESPECTIVE SIZES OF X AND Y,
001557,000032:                                                                                                  #                 USUALLY NUMERIC,  IE. 1, 2, 6, 18D ETC.               )
001558,000033: 
001559,000034: 
001560,000035:                                                                                                  #        EQUALS  OFTEN IMPLIES THE SHARING OF REGISTERS (DIFFERENT NAMES
001561,000036:                                                                                                  #                AND DIFFERENT DATA).  EXAMPLE.
001562,000037: 
001563,000038:                                                                                                  #                                        X       EQUALS  Y
001564,000039: 
001565,000040: 
001566,000041:                                                                                                  #        = MEANS THAT MULTIPLE NAMES HAVE BEEN GIVEN TO THE SAME DATA.
001567,000042:                                                                                                  #                (THIS IS LOGICAL EQUIVALENCE, NOT SHARING)  EXAMPLE.
001568,000043: 
001569,000044:                                                                                                  #                                        X       =       Y
001570,000045: 
001571,000046: 
001572,000047:                                                                                                  #        THE SIZE AND UTILIZATION OF AN ERASABLE ARE OFTEN INCLUDED IN
001573,000048:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMENTS IN THE FOLLOWING FORM.  M(SIZE)N.
001574,000049: 
001575,000050:                                                                                                  #                M REFERS TO THE MOBILITY OF THE ASSIGNMENT.
001576,000051:                                                                                                  #                     B   MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED BY BASIC
001577,000052:                                                                                                  #                         INSTRUCTIONS AND THUS IS E-BANK SENSITIVE.
001578,000053:                                                                                                  #                     I   MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED ONLY BY
001579,000054:                                                                                                  #                         INTERPRETIVE INSTRUCTIONS, AND IS THUS E-BANK
001580,000055:                                                                                                  #                         INSENSITIVE AND MAY APPEAR IN ANY E-BANK.
001581,000056: 
001582,000057:                                                                                                  #                SIZE IS THE NUMBER OF REGISTERS INCLUDED BY THE SYMBOL.
001583,000058: 
001584,000059:                                                                                                  #                N INDICATES THE NATURE OR PERMANENCE OF THE CONTENTS.
001585,000060:                                                                                                  #                     PL MEANS THAT THE CONTENTS ARE PAD LOADED.
001586,000061:                                                                                                  #                     DSP MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED FOR A DISPLAY.
001587,000062:                                                                                                  #                     PRM MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS PERMANENT, IE. IT
001588,000063:                                                                                                  #                         IS USED DURING THE ENTIRE MISSION FOR ONE
001589,000064:                                                                                                  #                         PURPOSE AND CANNOT BE SHARED.
001590,000065:                                                                                                  #                     TMP MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED TEMPORARILY OR
001591,000066:                                                                                                  #                         IS A SCRATCH REGISTER FOR THE ROUTINE TO WHICH
001592,000067:                                                                                                  #                         IT IS ASSIGNED.  THAT IS, IT NEED NOT BE SET
001593,000068:                                                                                                  #                         PRIOR TO INVOCATION OF THE ROUTINE NOR DOES IT
001594,000069:                                                                                                  #                         CONTAIN USEFUL OUTPUT TO ANOTHER ROUTINE.  THUS

Page 39 

001596,000071:                                                                                                  #                         IT MAY BE SHARED WITH ANY OTHER ROUTINE WHICH
001597,000072:                                                                                                  #                         IS NOT ACTIVE IN PARALLEL.
001598,000073:                                                                                                  #                     IN  MEANS INPUT TO THE ROUTINE AND IT IS PROBABLY
001599,000074:                                                                                                  #                         TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001600,000075:                                                                                                  #                     OUT MEANS OUTPUT FROM THE ROUTINE, PROBABLY
001601,000076:                                                                                                  #                         TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001602,000077:

001605,000080:                                                                                                  #        SPECIAL REGISTERS.
001606,000081: 
001607,000082: ???????                        A                  EQUALS   0                                     
001608,000083: ???????                        L                  EQUALS   1                                     #  L AND Q ARE BOTH CHANNELS AND REGISTERS.
001609,000084: ???????                        Q                  EQUALS   2                                     
001610,000085: ???????                        EBANK              EQUALS   3                                     
001611,000086: ???????                        FBANK              EQUALS   4                                     
001612,000087: ???????                        Z                  EQUALS   5                                     #  ADJACENT TO FBANK AND BBANK FOR DXCH Z
001613,000088: ???????                        BBANK              EQUALS   6                                     #  (DTCB) AND DXCH FBANK (DTCF).
001614,000089:                                                                                                  #  REGISTER 7 IS A ZERO-SOURCE, USED BY ZL.
001615,000090: 
001616,000091: ???????                        ARUPT              EQUALS   10                                    #  INTERRUPT STORAGE.
001617,000092: ???????                        LRUPT              EQUALS   11                                    
001618,000093: ???????                        QRUPT              EQUALS   12                                    
001619,000094: ???????                        SAMPTIME           EQUALS   13                                    #  SAMPLED TIME 1 & 2.
001620,000095: ???????                        ZRUPT              EQUALS   15                                    #  (13 AND 14 ARE SPARES.)

The trailing period in the line below is not visible in the printout, but I believe it is simply too faint to see. — RSB 2017.

002996,001471:                                                                                                  #  IS USED DURING CALLS TO THE EXECUTIVE AND WAITLIST - THE RUPTREGS ARE NOT.

003274,001749:                                                                                                  #  DESIRES TO BYPASS THE CHANNEL REPRESENTATION, HE SHOULD LOAD C31FLWRD   VIA V21 N01 TO THE VALUES SHOWN IN THE
003275,001750:                                                                                                  #  FOLLOWING TABLES:
003276,001751: 
003277,001752:                                                                                                  #     A VALUE      MEANING FOR CHANNEL 31                                     B VALUE      MEANING FOR CHANNEL 33
003278,001753: 
003279,001754:                                                                                                  #     0 OR 4       BITS 15,14, + 13 OF CHANNEL 31 ARE VALID                   0 OR 4       BITS 4 + 5 OF CHANNEL 33
003280,001755:                                                                                                  #     1            G&N CONTROL FREE                                           1 OR 5       OPTICS MODE CMC
003281,001756:                                                                                                  #     2            G&N CONTROL ATT. HOLD                                      2 OR 6       OPTICS MODE ZERO
003282,001757:                                                                                                  #     3            G&N CONTROL AUTO                                           3 OR 7       OPTICS MODE MANUAL
003283,001758:                                                                                                  #     5            SCS CONTROL FREE
